e000	"<LineBreak/><Bold>e000 Game Events Shown Here</Bold>
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>Active events show a green background. The game may only advance when a green background is displayed. Most often, the game advances by rolling die or clicking an image. However, the game lets you explore what may happen by showing inactive events. Inactive events have a gray background. To return to the current active event, select the active event button in the status bar per the image.
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>
                     <InlineUIContainer><Image Source='../images/Tutorial0.gif' Height='70'  Width='370'> </Image></InlineUIContainer>
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>
<InlineUIContainer><Button Name='Read_Rules' Content='Read Rules' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'> </Button></InlineUIContainer> or <InlineUIContainer><Button Name='Begin' Content='Begin Game' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'> </Button></InlineUIContainer>"
e000a	"<Bold>e000a Cal Arath - Barbarian Prince</Bold> <InlineUIContainer><Button Content='r200' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer> <InlineUIContainer><Button Content='r201' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/><Italic>Barbarian Prince</Italic> is a dungeon crawler, self-paced, solo game. You play the game in days. Each day starts with your selecting a daily action
 <InlineUIContainer><Button Content='r203' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>
, such as traveling to a new hex on the map. 
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>After all events are resolved for your daily action, you must eat your main evening meal as described in the food rules
 <InlineUIContainer><Button Content='r215' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>
, and if in a town, castle, or temple hex; you must also purchase lodging
 <InlineUIContainer><Button Content='r217' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>.
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>The game continues until either you are killed or 70 days (10 weeks) elapse. If you have not won before the 70 days ends, the game is automatically lost! You win if you collect 500gp.
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>You are Cal Arath, rightful heir to the throne of the Northlands Kingdom. 
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>Few humans match your skill with trusty Bonebiter -- Combat=8
<LineBreak/>Harsh northlands developed your powerful body -- Endurance=9. 
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>Counter Description is found by selecting <Bold>Help | Counter Description...</Bold> menu. Click image to continue.
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>
                                                <InlineUIContainer><Image Name='SetupShowStartingWealth' Source='../images/Tutorial1.gif' Height='150'  Width='150'> </Image></InlineUIContainer>"

e000c	"<Bold>e000c Random Wits and Wiles</Bold>
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>
In addition, you have a <Bold>wit and wiles</Bold> rating reflecting your ability to react quickly to situations, think your way out of trouble, and convince people to support your cause. 
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>
You wit and wiles will be shown in the status bar at the bottom.

e000d	"<Bold>e000d Manual Wits and Wiles</Bold>
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>
If you have played the game before and won, you may wish an extra challenge by using a wits and wiles rating one less than the previous value; if you lost in the previous game, use a wit and wiles one higher than the previous value.  
Change your wit and wiles by selecting buttons:
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/> 
<InlineUIContainer><Button Content='  -  ' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>
 or 
<InlineUIContainer><Button Content='  +  ' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>
 or click brain to continue.

e001	"<Bold>e001 The Adventure Begins</Bold>
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>
Evil events have overtaken your Northlands Kingdom. Your father, the old king, is dead - assassinated by rivals to the throne.  These usurpers now hold the palace with their mercenary royal guard. 
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>
You have escaped, and must collect 500 gold pieces to raise a force to smash them and retake your heritage. Furthermore, the usurpers have powerful friends overseas. If you can't return to take them out in ten weeks, their allies will arrive and you lose your kingdom forever. 
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>
At dawn, you roll out of the merchant wagons into a ditch, dust off your clothes, loosen your swordbelt, and get ready to start the first day of your adventure <InlineUIContainer><Button Content='r203' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>.
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>The original game is brutally difficult to win. The <Bold>recommended</Bold> fun game provides a random starting party, a random starting hex, food, and coins. Details can be viewed on the <Bold>File | Options...</Bold> menu where other game options can be selected. 
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>If you want different options, you must open the Options Dialog with <Bold>File | Options...</Bold> menu, and check the <Bold>AutoSetup</Bold> checkbox. Then, select <Bold>File | New</Bold> menu to start a new game with those options.
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>
<InlineUIContainer><Button Content='Original Game' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>
    or    
<InlineUIContainer><Button Content=' Fun Options ' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>"

or Weshor
 <InlineUIContainer><Button Content='1501' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>.

You must immediately roll once for each follower in your party, and any time the roll is greater than your wit and wiles, the follower will immediately desert you. 
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>
In addition, all monks and priests in the future will recognize the mark and will not join your party. You can never attempt an audience
 <InlineUIContainer><Button Content='r211' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>
 with the high priest of any temple marked on the map, but may with high priest of any secret unmarked temples that you find."

 5 - Voices of the gods gives a prophecy that seems to promise a treasure. See 
 <InlineUIContainer><Button Content='e147' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>.<LineBreak/>

In an astral vision, you see the gods striking down the usurpers to your throne and telling Northlands priests that your reign shall be holy. You will regain your throne and win the game if you can return alive to the Northlands, i.e., any hex north of the 
 <InlineUIContainer><Button Content='Tragoth River' FontFamily='Courier New'  FontSize='12'></Button></InlineUIContainer>

e228a	"<Bold>e228a True Love Separation</Bold>
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>In some cases, when you are believed dead, or imprisoned, you will be forcibly parted from the rest of your followers. Your true love will also be separated from you. As soon as you are set free, and reuniting is possible, roll two die at the end of the day. If the result is 10 or 11, you true love has finally found you. She rejoins the party. When you are reunited, roll two die again. If the results is 9 plus, she acquired a horse on her own journeys and brings that with her. If the result is 12, she acquired a winged mount (a Pegasus).
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>If the result is 12, you learn she died trying to find you, or trying to protect you. "
e228b	"<Bold>e228b The Eternal Triangle</Bold>
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>If you have a true love, and somehow acquire a second true love, a difficult situation exists. Since you are torn between the two neither of which is a true love, and the effects of true love no longer apply. 
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>You may lose all competing true loves save one. When only one remains, she becomes your real true love again.
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>The potential true loves will not desert you when you request it. However, whenever desertion would occur, roll one die. A 3 plus roll means the female remains with you that day like a true love. Otherwise she leaves. "

e343	"<Bold>e343 Victim Selection</Bold>
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>One character in your party is the victim or target of an attack. If your party is just you, then you are the target.
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>Otherwise, select characters in your party one by one in any order you choose. When you select a character, roll one die. If the result is six, the character is the target.
<LineBreak/><LineBreak/>Continue to do this going through the characters in your party until the target is selected. Continue from beginning if no target is selected until a target is confirmed."
